English

(With due devotion) we repeat the expression of adoration to our gurus
and likewise to their gurus;
and among these (latter),
we pray for the grace of the Primaeval Couple (N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa and Lakс╣гm─л ),
the twin ┼Ыeс╣г─лs1 of all the worlds
(so that they may be both the end to be attained by us
and the means of attaining it).

el gemelo ┼Ыeс╣г─лs 2 de todos los mundos

Having carefully studied the beautiful hymns
sung with delight in Tamil by seers,
we have come to understand the real meaning of the regions of the Upaniс╣гads which are otherwise difficult to comprehend -
seers known as Poygai Muni, Bhutamuni, Peyalvar, Kurugesan (Nammalvar) who was born on the banks of the cool Tamraparni, 5 Viс╣гс╣Зu cittan, the pure-minded Kulasekhara, our Pananathan, Thondaradippodi, the splendour that appeared in Mazhisai ( Tirumazhisai alvar) and the prince of Maс╣Еgai armed with sword and spear for making bright the path of the Vedas throughout the world.

рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рд╕-рдЯрд┐рдкреНрдкрдиреА

рдкреНрд░рдкреНрд░рддреНрддрд╛рд╡реН рдЕрдкреНрдпреН рдЖрдЪрд╛рд░реНрдпрдореН рдЕрдиреНрддрд░рд╛ рдорд╣рд╛рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рд╕рдВ рджреБрд╕реНрд╕рд╛рдзреНрдпрдореН рдЗрддрд┐ рд╡рджрдиреНрддрд┐ред

English

To those who venture to attain release from the bondage of saс╣Бs─Бra,
the ancient path indicated to us by the spotless Madhurakavi by his own example is the only safe7 path,

for while there is ┼Ъr─лkс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa, the great cowherd, who incarnated solely for the sake of his devotees to confer bliss on them, to be their refuge, to be their final goal, to stand in relation to them as mother, father, brother and so on,
to change their desire for the pleasures of this world into a desire for Himself, to remove all their sins, to show them infinite compassion, to reveal the truth, and so also to bring about in them a likeness to Himself - while there is ┼Ъr─лkс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa ever ready to do all this,8

he sought only the feet of the sage Satagopa (Namm─Бlv─Бr) who rendered in Tamil the truths contained in the Vedas which are otherwise hard to understand.

por su propio ejemplo es el ├║nico camino seguro 9,

que encarn├│ ├║nicamente por el bien de sus devotos para otorgarles la dicha, para ser su refugio, ser su objetivo final, para pararse en relaci├│n con ellos como madre, padre, hermano etc├йtera,

en un deseo por s├н mismo,

que hizo en tamil las verdades contenidas en los Vedas
que de otro modo son dif├нciles de entender.

English

It is said in the Smс╣Ыtis: “Kс╣гatrabandhu11 , who was the worst of sinners, and Puс╣Зс╕Нar─лka12 , the virtuous - both of them obtained mokс╣гa or release from bondage by virtue of their having ─Бc─Бryas.” It is thus declared that in the case of every one, the only means of securing mokс╣гa is to have an ─Бc─Бrya.

Espa├▒ol

Se dice en los Smс╣Ыtis:
“Kс╣гatrabandhu 13, que fue el peor de los pecadores,
y puс╣Зс╕Нar─лka 14, los virtuosos,
ambos obtuvieron mokс╣гa o liberaron de la esclavitud
por virtud de tener ─Бc─Бryas”.
Por lo tanto, se declara que en el caso de cada uno,
el ├║nico medio de asegurar mokс╣гa es tener un ─Бc─Бrya.

To the man desirous of mokс╣гa , the line of ─Бc─Бryas is stated in the ┼Ыruti15 to extend upward even to the Supreme Bhagav─Бn for purposes of meditation.

English

It follows from this that a man should bring his guru to light by way of the overflow of his supreme devotion to him under all conditions

and that the sacred mantra should not, for the sake of any material advantage,
be revealed to the fickle-minded who do not possess all the qualities prescribed for a disciple.

If the mantra is revealed to undeserving persons, its great value which is like that of a casket made of rubies containing a precious jewel will suffer and the guru’s spiritual greatness will also be adversely affected.

(6)

English

We shall come to new life again by bowing every day at the feet of the noble and generous N─Бthamuni,
who to his (two)37 loving disciples
who were like a trumpet and a conch (to proclaim the truth and to cow down the exponents of rival systems)
taught the art of music so that they might sing the sweet strains of the Tamil Veda
which had been long forgotten in the world

and who propagated in the world, for the pursuit of all,
the path of tapas (bhakti and prapatti).
In all the four regions of the world there is no one equal to us (because of this devotion of ours to N─Бthamuni).38

y que se propag├│ en el mundo, para la b├║squeda de todos, El camino de las tapas (Bhakti y Prapatti). En las cuatro regiones del mundo no hay nadie igual a nosotros (debido a esta devoci├│n nuestra a N─Бthamuni). 38
